<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>The following communications will be used from time to time in various corporate communication channels.
<U></U> </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ENERGY FACTOR PERSPECTIVE POST </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" ALIGN="center">


<TR>

<TD WIDTH="100%"></TD></TR>


<TR STYLE="page-break-inside:avoid ; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:1.00em; text-indent:-1.00em; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Hero Image</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:1pt">


<IMG SRC="g324352g0408234330421.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
</P></TD></TR>
</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Bart Cahir </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">04.08.2021 </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">ExxonMobil is the first company to file an application with the U.S. Environmental Protection Agency (EPA) to use new technologies to detect methane emissions
at oil and natural gas sites. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We are seeking approval with the EPA for an &#147;Alternate Means of Emissions Limitation&#148; so that we can use
airplanes equipped with detection technology to conduct flyover inspections over large areas. This would enable us to detect methane leaks across a broad geography and then send crews out to fix leaks more efficiently, ultimately enhancing the
compliance methods now required. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Existing regulations currently stipulate that individuals must travel from site to site with a hand-held camera to
inspect each piece of equipment. Through the EPA&#146;s process, we look forward to demonstrating how this alternative method works well across multiple distributed sites. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Effective methane detection technologies </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We hope this process
will pave the way for more flexibility for industry to deploy new technologies that can lead to a better result for everyone. Over time, technologies such as this can enable us to further reduce methane emissions from operations on private, state
and federal lands alike, while continuing to support thousands of jobs and drive billions of dollars in economic impact. We share the long-term goal of having the entire industry find and fix emission leaks most effectively. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">ExxonMobil has been at the forefront of looking for <U>new and better ways</U> to detect methane leaks, and this industry first is a concrete result that we
believe warrants adoption by regulators. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Reducing methane emissions </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Reducing leaks is part of our overall commitment to reduce methane emissions in our operations. Between 2016 and 2020 the company eliminated more than 67,000
tonnes of methane from its unconventional operations, and recently outlined plans for further reductions in methane intensity by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">40-50%</FONT> by 2025, compared to 2016. This includes our direct (Scope 1) and
indirect (Scope 2) emissions from our operated assets and is expected to result in a 40 to 50&nbsp;percent decrease in our absolute methane emissions globally. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We&#146;re working hard to reduce our own methane emissions, we&#146;ve long <U>advocated for federal
methane regulations</U> from both new and existing sources, and we&#146;re proud to be leading the way in deploying new technology. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Learn more about our
commitment to <U>reducing methane emissions</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Bart Cahir is Senior Vice President, Unconventional, ExxonMobil Upstream Oil&nbsp;&amp; Gas Company.
</I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">


<IMG SRC="g324352g0408234330701.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">


<IMG SRC="g324352g0408234330982.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P>
</DIV></Center>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

 </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD VALIGN="bottom" COLSPAN="3"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ENERGY FACTOR NEWSLETTER</B></P>

<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="top">Finding better ways to detect methane can enable us to further reduce our methane emissions. ExxonMobil is the first company to file an application seeking EPA approval to use new methane-detection technology in flyover inspections,
a proposal that could identify and fix leaks efficiently.</TD></TR>
</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>SOCIAL MEDIA </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Post Copy A: </B>We&#146;re seeking approval with the EPA for an &#147;Alternate Means of Emissions Limitation&#148; so that we can use airplanes equipped
with detection technology to conduct flyover inspections and detect methane leaks, which would enable us to fix methane leaks more efficiently. This industry first is a concrete result we believe warrants adoption by regulators. [LINK TO BLOG] </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Post Copy B: </B>We&#146;re seeking approval with the EPA for an &#147;Alternate Means of Emissions Limitation&#148; so we can use airplanes equipped with
detection technology to conduct flyover inspections. [LINK TO BLOG] </P>
</DIV></Center>
